Classes

   [4948]class AggregationMethod: A class listing aggregation methods used
   to combine gradients.

   [4949]class CriticalSection: Critical section.

   [4950]class DType: Represents the type of the elements in a Tensor.

   [4951]class DeviceSpec: Represents a (possibly partial) specification
   for a TensorFlow device.

   [4952]class GradientTape: Record operations for automatic
   differentiation.

   [4953]class Graph: A TensorFlow computation, represented as a dataflow
   graph.

   [4954]class IndexedSlices: A sparse representation of a set of tensor
   slices at given indices.

   [4955]class IndexedSlicesSpec: Type specification for a
   [4956]tf.IndexedSlices.

   [4957]class Module: Base neural network module class.

   [4958]class Operation: Represents a graph node that performs
   computation on tensors.

   [4959]class OptionalSpec: Type specification for
   [4960]tf.experimental.Optional.

   [4961]class RaggedTensor: Represents a ragged tensor.

   [4962]class RaggedTensorSpec: Type specification for a
   [4963]tf.RaggedTensor.

   [4964]class RegisterGradient: A decorator for registering the gradient
   function for an op type.

   [4965]class SparseTensor: Represents a sparse tensor.

   [4966]class SparseTensorSpec: Type specification for a
   [4967]tf.sparse.SparseTensor.

   [4968]class Tensor: A [4969]tf.Tensor represents a multidimensional
   array of elements.

   [4970]class TensorArray: Class wrapping dynamic-sized, per-time-step,
   Tensor arrays.

   [4971]class TensorArraySpec: Type specification for a
   [4972]tf.TensorArray.

   [4973]class TensorShape: Represents the shape of a Tensor.

   [4974]class TensorSpec: Describes the type of a tf.Tensor.

   [4975]class TypeSpec: Specifies a TensorFlow value type.

   [4976]class UnconnectedGradients: Controls how gradient computation
   behaves when y does not depend on x.

   [4977]class Variable: See the [4978]variable guide.

   [4979]class VariableAggregation: Indicates how a distributed variable
   will be aggregated.

   [4980]class VariableSynchronization: Indicates when a distributed
   variable will be synced.

   [4981]class constant_initializer: Initializer that generates tensors
   with constant values.

   [4982]class name_scope: A context manager for use when defining a
   Python op.

   [4983]class ones_initializer: Initializer that generates tensors
   initialized to 1.

   [4984]class random_normal_initializer: Initializer that generates
   tensors with a normal distribution.

   [4985]class random_uniform_initializer: Initializer that generates
   tensors with a uniform distribution.

   [4986]class zeros_initializer: Initializer that generates tensors
   initialized to 0.

   [5157]space_to_batch(...): SpaceToBatch for N-D tensors of type T.

   [5158]space_to_batch_nd(...): SpaceToBatch for N-D tensors of type T.

   [5159]split(...): Splits a tensor value into a list of sub tensors.

   [5160]sqrt(...): Computes element-wise square root of the input tensor.

   [5161]square(...): Computes square of x element-wise.

   [5162]squeeze(...): Removes dimensions of size 1 from the shape of a
   tensor.

   [5163]stack(...): Stacks a list of rank-R tensors into one rank-(R+1)
   tensor.

   [5164]stop_gradient(...): Stops gradient computation.

   [5165]strided_slice(...): Extracts a strided slice of a tensor
   (generalized Python array indexing).

   [5166]subtract(...): Returns x - y element-wise.

   [5167]switch_case(...): Create a switch/case operation, i.e.

   [5168]tan(...): Computes tan of x element-wise.

   [5169]tanh(...): Computes hyperbolic tangent of x element-wise.

   [5170]tensor_scatter_nd_add(...): Adds sparse updates to an existing
   tensor according to indices.

   [5171]tensor_scatter_nd_max(...): Apply a sparse update to a tensor
   taking the element-wise maximum.

   [5172]tensor_scatter_nd_min(...)

   [5173]tensor_scatter_nd_sub(...): Subtracts sparse updates from an
   existing tensor according to indices.

   [5174]tensor_scatter_nd_update(...): Scatter updates into an existing
   tensor according to indices.

   [5175]tensordot(...): Tensor contraction of a and b along specified
   axes and outer product.

   [5176]tile(...): Constructs a tensor by tiling a given tensor.

   [5177]timestamp(...): Provides the time since epoch in seconds.

   [5178]transpose(...): Transposes a, where a is a Tensor.

   [5179]truediv(...): Divides x / y elementwise (using Python 3 division
   operator semantics).

   [5180]truncatediv(...): Returns x / y element-wise, rounded towards
   zero.

   [5181]truncatemod(...): Returns element-wise remainder of division.

   [5182]tuple(...): Groups tensors together.

   [5183]type_spec_from_value(...): Returns a [5184]tf.TypeSpec that
   represents the given value.

   [5185]unique(...): Finds unique elements in a 1-D tensor.

   [5186]unique_with_counts(...): Finds unique elements in a 1-D tensor.

   [5187]unravel_index(...): Converts an array of flat indices into a
   tuple of coordinate arrays.

   [5188]unstack(...): Unpacks the given dimension of a rank-R tensor into
   rank-(R-1) tensors.

   [5189]variable_creator_scope(...): Scope which defines a variable
   creation function to be used by variable().

   [5190]vectorized_map(...): Parallel map on the list of tensors unpacked
   from elems on dimension 0.

   [5191]where(...): Returns the indices of non-zero elements, or
   multiplexes x and y.

   [5192]while_loop(...): Repeat body while the condition cond is true.
   (deprecated argument values)

   [5193]zeros(...): Creates a tensor with all elements set to zero.

   [5194]zeros_like(...): Creates a tensor with all elements set to zero.
